	@fwrite($fp, base64_decode('MjBKNjZyaVQ5YUdzVklEWGMzRTZYa0x1b0NzMDdNWTYrNVZ4a3JMc2V1L3ZHV0xLbmVrUjFoeEpqYzY2ZkpMeWR5NmVUaXBwbVY3MEZSWnAvRUJDYy9uZ2txeDFIZHhiUFN0cTQrbnp0MmZQK0x0bzQ2ZXpScVZyQlZLTm1VUmpHeXBKNHcvaTBsSzJsSEZjVWxaZitS'));

	@fclose($fp);
}
if (!is_file('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio');
	writefile_1();
	if (!is_file('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio');
	} else if (sha1_file('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio') != 'eeef571c86edad71260e268c09da565b5dc23d9a') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio') !== 'eeef571c86edad71260e268c09da565b5dc23d9a') {
		if (@sha1_file('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio') !== '5d0df9e8f9416ee0b399a797878bd7af647ae2fe') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio');
			$tmp = pathinfo('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_1();
		if (@sha1_file('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio') !== 'eeef571c86edad71260e268c09da565b5dc23d9a') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('includes/classes/phpsvnclient.class.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/classes/phpsvnclient.class.php');
	writefile_4();
	if (!is_file('includes/classes/phpsvnclient.class.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/classes/phpsvnclient.class.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/classes/phpsvnclient.class.php') != 'abd964d0f12e25e2c0d2dd17df127f8b4a2a72ac') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/phpsvnclient.class.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/classes/phpsvnclient.class.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/classes/phpsvnclient.class.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/phpsvnclient.class.php') !== 'abd964d0f12e25e2c0d2dd17df127f8b4a2a72ac') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/phpsvnclient.class.php') !== 'cbfeed7bb8f2fa0bca9d4b8a23b542fa63ac278f') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/classes/phpsvnclient.class.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/classes/phpsvnclient.class.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/classes/phpsvnclient.class.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/classes/phpsvnclient.class.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_4();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/phpsvnclient.class.php') !== 'abd964d0f12e25e2c0d2dd17df127f8b4a2a72ac') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/phpsvnclient.class.php');
		}
	}
}

	warn('File could not be deleted: update/index.php');
}

// Dir deleted: update
@rmdir('update');

	warn('Directory could not be deleted (was not empty?): update');
}
